\subsection{Detailed Description}
Utility methods for String operations. All methods in the \hyperlink{class_ultimate_1_1_utilities_1_1_string_utils}{String\+Utils} are Null safe.

Gets a substring from the given string without raising exceptions. 

A negative start position can be used to start characters from the end of the String. Null string will return Null and Empty (\char`\"{}\char`\"{}) string will return Empty (\char`\"{}\char`\"{}) String. 

String\+Utils.\+Substring(null, $\ast$) = null
